# Workforce AI Platform \- Enterprise Architecture & Implementation Guide

Comprehensive documentation pack for Workforce AI.

# **1\. Executive Summary**

## **Executive Summary \- Detail 1**

Purpose:  
This section defines enterprise-grade implementation guidance for the Workforce AI platform.

Key Topics:  
\- Architectural principles  
\- Design decisions  
\- Trade-offs  
\- Scalability concerns  
\- Security considerations  
\- Development standards

Implementation Guidance:  
Use clean architecture, domain-driven modular boundaries, strict TypeScript settings,  
structured logging, validation, observability, and automated testing. All AI interactions  
must return structured outputs and never directly mutate business data without validation.

Engineering Standards:  
\- NestJS modules per domain  
\- Prisma as data access layer  
\- DTO validation  
\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

# **2\. Product Vision**

## **Product Vision \- Detail 1**

Purpose:  
This section defines enterprise-grade implementation guidance for the Workforce AI platform.

Key Topics:  
\- Architectural principles  
\- Design decisions  
\- Trade-offs  
\- Scalability concerns  
\- Security considerations  
\- Development standards

Implementation Guidance:  
Use clean architecture, domain-driven modular boundaries, strict TypeScript settings,  
structured logging, validation, observability, and automated testing. All AI interactions  
must return structured outputs and never directly mutate business data without validation.

Engineering Standards:  
\- NestJS modules per domain  
\- Prisma as data access layer  
\- DTO validation  
\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

This section defines enterprise-grade implementation guidance for the Workforce AI platform.

Implementation Guidance:  
Use clean architecture, domain-driven modular boundaries, strict TypeScript settings,  
structured logging, validation, observability, and automated testing. All AI interactions  
must return structured outputs and never directly mutate business data without validation.

Engineering Standards:  
\- NestJS modules per domain  
\- Prisma as data access layer  
\- DTO validation  
\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

Purpose:  
This section defines enterprise-grade implementation guidance for the Workforce AI platform.

Key Topics:  
\- Architectural principles  
\- Design decisions  
\- Trade-offs  
\- Scalability concerns  
\- Security considerations  
\- Development standards

Implementation Guidance:  
Use clean architecture, domain-driven modular boundaries, strict TypeScript settings,  
structured logging, validation, observability, and automated testing. All AI interactions  
must return structured outputs and never directly mutate business data without validation.

Engineering Standards:  
\- NestJS modules per domain  
\- Prisma as data access layer  
\- DTO validation  
\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

\- Trade-offs  
\- Scalability concerns  
\- Security considerations  
\- Development standards

Implementation Guidance:  
Use clean architecture, domain-driven modular boundaries, strict TypeScript settings,  
structured logging, validation, observability, and automated testing. All AI interactions  
must return structured outputs and never directly mutate business data without validation.

Engineering Standards:  
\- NestJS modules per domain  
\- Prisma as data access layer  
\- DTO validation  
\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

Implementation Guidance:  
Use clean architecture, domain-driven modular boundaries, strict TypeScript settings,  
structured logging, validation, observability, and automated testing. All AI interactions  
must return structured outputs and never directly mutate business data without validation.

Engineering Standards:  
\- NestJS modules per domain  
\- Prisma as data access layer  
\- DTO validation  
\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

## **System Architecture \- Detail 10**

This section defines enterprise-grade implementation guidance for the Workforce AI platform.

Key Topics:  
\- Architectural principles  
\- Design decisions  
\- Trade-offs  
\- Scalability concerns  
\- Security considerations  
\- Development standards

Implementation Guidance:  
Use clean architecture, domain-driven modular boundaries, strict TypeScript settings,  
structured logging, validation, observability, and automated testing. All AI interactions  
must return structured outputs and never directly mutate business data without validation.

Engineering Standards:  
\- NestJS modules per domain  
\- Prisma as data access layer  
\- DTO validation  
\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs

\- Security considerations  
\- Development standards

Implementation Guidance:  
Use clean architecture, domain-driven modular boundaries, strict TypeScript settings,  
structured logging, validation, observability, and automated testing. All AI interactions  
must return structured outputs and never directly mutate business data without validation.

Engineering Standards:  
\- NestJS modules per domain  
\- Prisma as data access layer  
\- DTO validation  
\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

\- Trade-offs  
\- Scalability concerns  
\- Security considerations  
\- Development standards

Implementation Guidance:  
Use clean architecture, domain-driven modular boundaries, strict TypeScript settings,  
structured logging, validation, observability, and automated testing. All AI interactions  
must return structured outputs and never directly mutate business data without validation.

Engineering Standards:  
\- NestJS modules per domain  
\- Prisma as data access layer  
\- DTO validation  
\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

Use clean architecture, domain-driven modular boundaries, strict TypeScript settings,  
structured logging, validation, observability, and automated testing. All AI interactions  
must return structured outputs and never directly mutate business data without validation.

Engineering Standards:  
\- NestJS modules per domain  
\- Prisma as data access layer  
\- DTO validation  
\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

\- DTO validation  
\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

## **Organization & RBAC Design \- Detail 5**

Purpose:  
This section defines enterprise-grade implementation guidance for the Workforce AI platform.

Key Topics:  
\- Architectural principles  
\- Design decisions  
\- Trade-offs  
\- Scalability concerns  
\- Security considerations  
\- Development standards

Implementation Guidance:  
Use clean architecture, domain-driven modular boundaries, strict TypeScript settings,  
structured logging, validation, observability, and automated testing. All AI interactions  
must return structured outputs and never directly mutate business data without validation.

Engineering Standards:  
\- NestJS modules per domain  
\- Prisma as data access layer  
\- DTO validation  
\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

Key Topics:  
\- Architectural principles  
\- Design decisions  
\- Trade-offs  
\- Scalability concerns  
\- Security considerations  
\- Development standards

Implementation Guidance:  
Use clean architecture, domain-driven modular boundaries, strict TypeScript settings,  
structured logging, validation, observability, and automated testing. All AI interactions  
must return structured outputs and never directly mutate business data without validation.

Engineering Standards:  
\- NestJS modules per domain  
\- Prisma as data access layer  
\- DTO validation  
\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

Implementation Guidance:  
Use clean architecture, domain-driven modular boundaries, strict TypeScript settings,  
structured logging, validation, observability, and automated testing. All AI interactions  
must return structured outputs and never directly mutate business data without validation.

Engineering Standards:  
\- NestJS modules per domain  
\- Prisma as data access layer  
\- DTO validation  
\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

\- Development standards

Implementation Guidance:  
Use clean architecture, domain-driven modular boundaries, strict TypeScript settings,  
structured logging, validation, observability, and automated testing. All AI interactions  
must return structured outputs and never directly mutate business data without validation.

Engineering Standards:  
\- NestJS modules per domain  
\- Prisma as data access layer  
\- DTO validation  
\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

## **Tool Calling Framework \- Detail 2**

\- Architectural principles  
\- Design decisions  
\- Trade-offs  
\- Scalability concerns  
\- Security considerations  
\- Development standards

Implementation Guidance:

must return structured outputs and never directly mutate business data without validation.

\- Trade-offs  
\- Scalability concerns  
\- Security considerations  
\- Development standards

Implementation Guidance:  
Use clean architecture, domain-driven modular boundaries, strict TypeScript settings,  
structured logging, validation, observability, and automated testing. All AI interactions  
must return structured outputs and never directly mutate business data without validation.

Engineering Standards:  
\- NestJS modules per domain  
\- Prisma as data access layer  
\- DTO validation  
\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

\- NestJS modules per domain  
\- Prisma as data access layer  
\- DTO validation  
\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

This section defines enterprise-grade implementation guidance for the Workforce AI platform.

Key Topics:  
\- Architectural principles  
\- Design decisions  
\- Trade-offs  
\- Scalability concerns  
\- Security considerations  
\- Development standards

Implementation Guidance:  
Use clean architecture, domain-driven modular boundaries, strict TypeScript settings,  
structured logging, validation, observability, and automated testing. All AI interactions  
must return structured outputs and never directly mutate business data without validation.

Engineering Standards:  
\- NestJS modules per domain  
\- Prisma as data access layer  
\- DTO validation  
\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

Use clean architecture, domain-driven modular boundaries, strict TypeScript settings,  
structured logging, validation, observability, and automated testing. All AI interactions  
must return structured outputs and never directly mutate business data without validation.

Engineering Standards:  
\- NestJS modules per domain  
\- Prisma as data access layer  
\- DTO validation  
\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

\- Trade-offs  
\- Scalability concerns  
\- Security considerations  
\- Development standards

Implementation Guidance:  
Use clean architecture, domain-driven modular boundaries, strict TypeScript settings,  
structured logging, validation, observability, and automated testing. All AI interactions  
must return structured outputs and never directly mutate business data without validation.

Engineering Standards:  
\- NestJS modules per domain  
\- Prisma as data access layer  
\- DTO validation  
\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

must return structured outputs and never directly mutate business data without validation.

Engineering Standards:  
\- NestJS modules per domain  
\- Prisma as data access layer  
\- DTO validation  
\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

Use clean architecture, domain-driven modular boundaries, strict TypeScript settings,  
structured logging, validation, observability, and automated testing. All AI interactions  
must return structured outputs and never directly mutate business data without validation.

Engineering Standards:  
\- NestJS modules per domain  
\- Prisma as data access layer  
\- DTO validation  
\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

\- Development standards

Implementation Guidance:  
Use clean architecture, domain-driven modular boundaries, strict TypeScript settings,  
structured logging, validation, observability, and automated testing. All AI interactions  
must return structured outputs and never directly mutate business data without validation.

Engineering Standards:  
\- NestJS modules per domain  
\- Prisma as data access layer  
\- DTO validation  
\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

\- Prisma as data access layer  
\- DTO validation  
\- RBAC enforcement  
\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture

Purpose:

Key Topics:  
\- Architectural principles  
\- Design decisions  
\- Trade-offs  
\- Scalability concerns  
\- Security considerations  
\- Development standards

Implementation Guidance:  
Use clean architecture, domain-driven modular boundaries, strict TypeScript settings,  
structured logging, validation, observability, and automated testing. All AI interactions  
must return structured outputs and never directly mutate business data without validation.

Engineering Standards:  
\- NestJS modules per domain  
\- Prisma as data access layer  
\- DTO validation

\- Audit logging  
\- Provider abstraction for LLMs  
\- Ollama-first architecture
